    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[ProductNameEn], [p].[ProductNameFr], [p].[ProductUrl], [p].[TypeId], [p].[isHotSale], [p].[isManufactured]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [ProductTypes] AS [p0] ON [t].[TypeId] = [p0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImgs] AS [p1] ON [t].[Id] = [p1].[ProductID]
LEFT JOIN [ProductDescs] AS [p2] ON [t].[Id] = [p2].[ProductID]
LEFT JOIN [ProductProperties] AS [p3] ON [t].[Id] = [p3].[ProductID]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [p0].[Id], [p1].[Id], [p2].[Id]
